<script>!function(d,s,id){var js,fjs=d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0],p=/^http:/.test(d.location)?'http':'https';if(!d.getElementById(id)){js=d.createElement(s);js.id=id;js.src=p+'://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js';fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js,fjs);}}(document, 'script', 'twitter-wjs');</script>

<script>
    $(function(){
        // 検索モーダル
        var $html = $('html');
        var $overlay = $('.modalOverlay');
        var $content = $('.modalContent').css({
            'max-height' : '80vh',
            'overflow' : 'auto',
            'width' : 1000 + 'px'
        });
        var closeModal = function() {
            // モーダル消す
            $overlay.add($content).fadeOut();
            // 背景のスクロール許可
            $html.css('overflow','');
        };
        $overlay.on('click', closeModal);
        $('.btnSearch').on('click',function(){
            // 背景のスクロール禁止
            $html.css('overflow','hidden');
            // モーダル表示位置を調整する
            $overlay.fadeIn();
            $content.css({
                top: ($(window).height() - $content.outerHeight()) / 2,
                left: ($(window).width() - $content.outerWidth()) / 2
            }).fadeIn();
        });
        $('#search').submit(function(){
                        setTimeout(function(){
                let form = $('#search');
                form.off('submit');
                form.submit();
            }, 500);
            $('.modalContent').fadeOut(300);
            $('.modalOverlay').fadeOut(300);
            $('#is-loading').fadeIn(300);
            $('#loading').fadeIn(300);
            return false;
        });
        $('form#search select[name="year"]').change(function () {
            load_section();
        });
        $('form#search input[name="category[]"]').change(function() {
            load_section();
        });
        $('.checkArea ul li input#all').on("click",function(){
            $(this).parents('ul').find('input').prop("checked", $(this).prop("checked"));
        });
        $('.checkArea ul li.col1 input').on("click",function(){
            $(this).parents('ul').find('input').prop("checked", $(this).prop("checked"));
        });
        $('.checkArea ul li input').on("click",function(){
            var checked = true;
            $(this).parents('ul').find('input').not(':first').each(function() {
                if ($(this).prop("checked") == false) {
                    checked = false;
                    return false;
                }
            });
            $(this).parents('ul').find('input.all').eq(0).prop("checked",checked);
        });
        $('#tba').on("click",function(){
            if ($(this).prop("checked") == true) {
                $('#begin option:eq(0)').attr("selected","selected");
                $('#end option:eq(0)').attr("selected","selected");
            }
        });

        // セクション表示スライダ
        var sectionAbove  = $('.pageAboveNavArea .sectionNav ul'),
            sectionBottom = $('.pagebottomNavArea .sectionNav ul');
        sectionAbove.children('li:first-child').show();
        var tSlider = sectionAbove.bxSlider({
            infiniteLoop: false,
            speed: 500,
            auto: false,
            ticker: false,
            pager: false,
            adaptiveHeight: true,
            touchEnabled: false,
            moveSlides: 3,
            maxSlides: 12,
            hideControlOnEnd: true,
            slideWidth: 80,
            onSliderLoad: function(){
                $('.nowloading').hide();
                sectionAbove.children('li').show();
                sectionAbove.goToSlide(0);
                $('.sectionElement0').addClass('active');
            }
        });

        sectionBottom.children('li:first-child').show();
        var bSlider = sectionBottom.bxSlider({
            infiniteLoop: false,
            speed: 500,
            auto: false,
            ticker: false,
            pager: false,
            adaptiveHeight: true,
            touchEnabled: false,
            moveSlides: 3,
            maxSlides: 12,
            hideControlOnEnd: true,
            slideWidth: 80,
            onSliderLoad: function(currentIndex){
                sectionBottom.children('li').show();
                sectionBottom.goToSlide(0);
                $('.sectionElement0').addClass('active');
            }
        });

        // カレンダーを表示
        load_calendar({
            'y' : JSON.parse('"2024"'),
            'm' : JSON.parse('"2"')
        });
        load_section();
    });

    var flag_load_calendar;
    function load_calendar(params) {
        if(typeof params === 'undefined') params = false;
        if(flag_load_calendar) {return;}
        flag_load_calendar = true;
        var category = JSON.parse('["j1"]');
        var club = JSON.parse('[]');
        var year = ("y" in params) ? params['y'] : JSON.parse('"2024"');
        var month = ("m" in params) ? params['m'] : JSON.parse('["02","03","04","05","06","07","08","09","10","11"]');
        var data = {
            "category" : category,
            "club" : club,
            "year" : year,
            "month" : month
        };
        $.ajax({
            type: 'GET',
            url: '/api/match/calendar',
            cache: true,
            dataType: 'html',
            xhrFields: {
                withCredentials: true
            },
            data: data,
        }).done(function(data) {
            $('#subCalendar').html(data);
        }).always(function(data) {
            flag_load_calendar = false;
        });
    }

    function getUrlParameter(sParam) {
        var sPageURL = window.location.search.substring(1),
            sURLVariables = sPageURL.split('&'),
            sParameterName,
            i;

        for (i = 0; i < sURLVariables.length; i++) {
            sParameterName = sURLVariables[i].split('=');

            if (sParameterName[0] === sParam) {
                return sParameterName[1] === undefined ? true : decodeURIComponent(sParameterName[1]);
            }
        }
    }

    function load_section() {
        var year = $('form#search select[name="year"]').val();
        var category = $('form#search input[name="category[]"]:checked').map(function(){
            return $(this).val();
        }).get();
        if (year == '' || category.length != 1) {
            $('form#search select#section').parents('.checkArea').fadeOut();
            $('form#search select#section option').remove();
            return;
        }
        $.ajax({
            type: 'GET',
            url: '/api/match/section.json',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'json',
            xhrFields: {
                withCredentials: true
            },
            data: {
                'year':year,
                'category':category.shift()
            },
        }).done(function(data) {
            if (data == undefined) {
                $('form#search select#section').parents('.checkArea').fadeOut();
                $('form#search select#section option').remove();
                return;
            }
            $('form#search select#section').parents('.checkArea').fadeIn();
            var html = '<option value="">-</option>';
            for(var key in data) {
                html += "<option value=" + data[key]['key']  + ">" +data[key]['value'] + "</option>"
            }
            $('form#search select#section').html(html);
            var selected = getUrlParameter('section');
            $('form#search select#section  option[value="'+selected+'"]').attr('selected', true);
        }).always(function(data) {
            flag_load_calendar = false;
        });
    }

    function select_club(obj) {
        index = obj.selectedIndex;
        if (index != 0){
            club_name = obj.options[index].value;
            url_string = '';
            href = url_string+'/'+club_name;
            location.href = href;
        }
    }
    function winner_link(gameDate, teamid, url = '/winner/purchase/', gameKindId, forceService = null) {
        // Cookie取得
        get_service(gameDate, teamid, gameKindId, forceService).done(function (data) {
            // 成功 ディープリンクに遷移
            // alert(data.url+'に遷移予定');
            // window.location.href = data.url;
            if (data.service != null) {
                window.location.href = data.url;
                // window.open(data.url, '_blank');
            } else {
                window.location.href = url + '?gameDate=' + gameDate + '&teamid=' + teamid + '&gameKindId=' + gameKindId + '&forceService=' + forceService;
            }
        }).fail(function (){
            // 失敗
        });
    }

    function get_service(game_date = null, team_id = null, game_kind_id = null, force_service = null) {
        let data = {
            'url': encodeURI(decodeURI(location.href)),
            'game_date': game_date,
            'team_id': team_id,
            'game_kind_id': game_kind_id,
            'force_service': force_service
        };

        return $.ajax({
            url: '/api/winner/getservice/',
            type: 'GET',
            cache: false,
//        async: false, // 同期
            dataType: 'json',
//        processData: false,
//        contentType: 'application/json; charset=utf-8',
            data: JSON.stringify(data),
            xhrFields: {
                withCredentials: true
            },
//        headers: {
//            'X-CSRF-TOKEN': $('meta[name="csrf-token"]').attr('value'),
//        },
            timeout: 1000
        });
    }

    function set_service(service) {
        let data = {
            'url': encodeURI(decodeURI(location.href)),
            'service': service
        };
        return $.ajax({
            url: '/api/winner/setservice/',
            type: 'POST',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'json',
            processData: false,
            contentType: 'application/json; charset=utf-8',
            data: JSON.stringify(data),
            xhrFields: {
                withCredentials: true
            },
            headers: {
                'X-CSRF-TOKEN': $('meta[name="csrf-token"]').attr('value'),
            },
            timeout: 1000
        });
    }
</script>

</body>
